i am speaking from a media house in Delhi
 
 
 " lakhanu kii ek basti main bani bilkul saadhaaran-si teen-manzila imaarat main isi yuvati jaisi 70 anya ladkiyaan bhi maujuud hai, jo bilkul isi tarah kii baatcheet kar rahi hai
 On the other side of the phone line are voters, or people who can influence the rural electorate, from whom the callers are hoping to garner support for their client Akhilesh Yadav
 lekin in choleron se kaha gaya he ki ve kisi ko bhi khud kaa parichay uttar pradesh ke mukhyamantri ke numayande ke taur par na den
 Instead, all of them are saying that they represent a Delhi-based media house, and are conducting an election survey
 
 
 lekin unke sawaalon or baatcheet main yah jaanane kii koshish kii ja rahi he kisi gaanv yaa booth ke ilaake main koi khaas jati yaa samudaay akhilesh yadav ke paksh main yaa khilaaf to nahin he
 'troublesome' information is given to a group of 700 working people on the ground, whose job is to try to tilt the people towards Akhilesh Yadav by visiting those areas, and yes, these people Has also been explicitly told not to tell anyone what they are working for
 yah ranneeti - dhake-chhipe tareeke se maan-manouvval kii niti - akhilesh yadav ke liye hazaron mile dur baithe steve jarding ne taiyaar kii he, jo harvard uniwarsity ke kennedy skool of gavarnence main lekturer hai

 " iske bajaay ve sabhi kah rahi hai ki ve dilli sthit ek media house kii pratinidhi hai, or ek chunavi survey kar rahi hai
 
 
 But in his questions and conversations, it is being tried to know whether any particular caste or community in any village or booth area is in favor or against Akhilesh Yadav
 'musiibat paidaa karne vaali' soochnaaon kii jaankaree jamini taur par kaam kar rahe 700 logon ke group ko de di jaati he, jinka kaam un ilaakon kaa daura kar logon kaa jhukaav akhilesh yadav kii ore karne kii koshish karnaa he, or haa, in logon ko bhi saaf-saaf kah diya gaya he ki ve kisi ko na bataaen ki ve kiske liye kaam kar rahe hai
 This strategy - a covertly man-of-the-man policy - has been devised thousands of miles away by Steve Jarding, a lecturer at Harvard University's Kennedy School of Governance, for Akhilesh Yadav
 steve jarding ke ek shishy advait vikram singh ne hi unka parichay agast main akhilesh yadav se karavaaya tha, or tabhi se yah america vidwaan mukhyamantri ke liye ranneeti taiyaar karne main madad kar rahe hai, jisamen akhilesh kii unke pita mulaayam singh yadav se hui zordaar jang bhi shaamil he
 Some believe that during the Uttar Pradesh election campaign, Akhilesh Yadav took the decision to project himself as a pro-development leader who transcends caste boundaries
 advait vikram singh ne NDTV ko bataaya, "yah steve kaa vyaktigat akalan tha ki akhilesh yadav kaa naam hi sandesh ban janaa chahie
 
 
 " haalanki isi dauraan isi imaarat main kinhin anya kamaron main, jinamein se kuch main hamen bhi le jaaya gaya, jati samikarnon ko baariki se sanbhaalane kaa kaam bhi jari he, kyonki yah vah kaam he, jo is kshetra main hone vaale kisi bhi chunaav main behad ahm bhoomika nibhaataa he, or jise chunaav se alag nahin kiya ja saktaa he

 Avnish Kumar Rai, appearing at the age of 45-46, told, "I want to know why some faction is against us

 " majlis-e-ittehadul Muslimeen MLA Akbaruddin Owaisi was sent to 14 days judicial custody by a magistrate in Nirmal town of Adilabad district
 ovaisi ke khilaaf kathith bhadakaau bhaashan dene ke aarope main kai maamle darj kiye gaye hai
 It is said that Akbaruddin Owaisi was produced before the magistrate at half past five in the morning and then sent to judicial custody
 magistrate ne police se ovaisi ko subah saadhe 10 baje adaalat main pesh karne ke liye bhi kaha
 Owaisi was taken to the Nirmal City Police Station
 samajha jaataa he ki unki yachika andhra pradesh adaalat main aaj sunwaayee ke liye soochibaddh he
 The MIM MLA was arrested on Tuesday
 giraftaar se ek din pehle hi vah landan se laute the or swasthya sambandhi jaanch ke liye unhen aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya tha
 He was later detained
 tippaniyan After the arrest of the MIM leader, the state government imposed prohibitory orders in the city to maintain law and order
 hyderabad or aadilabad main aihtiyaat ke taur par atirikt suraksha bal tainaat kiye gaye hai
 Owaisi is the leader of MIM in the Andhra Pradesh Legislative Assembly
 un par aadilabad main charminar ilaake ke vivaadaaspad bhagyalakshmi mandir ko lekar kathith bhadakaau bhaashan dene ke aarope main maamla darj kiya gaya he
 a complaint has been lodged against him in police stations of Hyderabad and various parts of the state on the charge of giving similar speeches
 bataaya jaataa he ki akbaruddin ovaisi ko subah saadhe paanch baje magistrate ke samaksh pesh kiya gaya or phir unhen nyaayik hiraasat main bhej diya gaya
 The magistrate also asked the police to produce Owaisi in the court at 10:30 am
 ovaisi ko nirmal shahar police thana le jaaya gaya
 His petition is understood to be listed for hearing in an Andhra Pradesh court today
 emm ke vidhayak ko mangalvaar ko giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 He returned from London a day before his arrest and was hospitalized for a health check-up
 baad main unhen hiraasat main liya gaya
 The comments emm netaa kii giraftaar ke baad rajya sarkaar ne kanoon-vyavastha banaae rakhane ke liye shahar main nishedhagna lagu kar di
 Additional security forces have been deployed in Hyderabad and Adilabad as a precautionary measure
 ovaisi andhra pradesh vidhansabha main emm ke netaa hai
 He has been booked for allegedly making inflammatory speeches regarding the controversial Bhagyalakshmi temple in Charminar area in Adilabad
 aise hi bhaashan dene ke aarope main unke khilaaf hyderabad or rajya ke vibhinn hisson ke police thanon main shikaayat darj karai gai he

 Employee's Pension Scheme: supreme court(supreme Court) ne centre sarkaar ko bada jhatka dete hue nijee sector( Private Employee's) ke lakhon karmchaariyon ko baari raahat di he
 With the Supreme Court ruling, the pension of millions of employees who contribute to the Employees Provident Fund (EPF) can increase manifold in one stroke
 darasal karmchaaree bhavishya nidhi sanghathan(epfo) ne karmchaariyon kii pension ke liye unki adhiktam selleri 15 hajaar rupee tay kii thi
 Meaning to say, even though your salary is more than 15 thousand rupees per month, your pension will be calculated on maximum salary of 15 thousand rupees only
 magar supreme court ne ipiefo kii ore se nirdhaarit is selleri-seemaa ko tod diya he
 Now the pension of the employees will be calculated on the basis of last salary i
e
 highest salary
 jisase is faisle se karmchaariyon ko kai guna zyada pension milegi
 Here, it is necessary to contribute to the Employees Provident Fund for 10 years to get the pension
 vahiin 20 saal kii sarvice puri karne par do saal kaa vettege miltaa he
 As a hallmark, suppose a person named Vivek is employed
 vah 33 saal kii naukari puri karte hai
 His last salary is 50 thousand rupees
 puraani vyavastha ke tahat inaki pension kii gananaa adhiktam 15 hajaar rupee kii selleri par hi hoti
 Thus, they would have received only Rs 7,500 pension under the formula (formula: 33 years + 2 = 35 / 70 x15,000)
 yani puraani vyavastha ke tahat vivek ko saadhe saat hajaar rupee masik pension milti
 Whereas now, after adding the pension according to the last salary in the new system, they will get a pension of 25000 thousand rupees
 dekhen ganit- ( 33 saal + 2= 35 / 70 x50,000=25000
 Please tell here that according to the rule of EPFO, if you have contributed while serving 20 years or more, then two more years are added to your service
 is prakaar vivek ne bhale hi 33 saal kii naukari puri kii, magar pension kii gananaa 35 saal ke liye hui
 Thus Vivek's salary increases by 333 percent
